ASU 2017-12 amends the hedge accounting recognition and presentation requirements in ASC 815. In summary, ASU 2017-12 eliminates the concept of separately recognizing periodic hedge ineffectiveness for cash flow and net investment hedges. The Bank has certain notional amounts of interest rate swaps which are considered cash flow hedges under current guidance and had previously recognized approximately $1.5 million as a charge to income for the calculated amount of hedge ineffectiveness as of and for the three-month period ended June 30, 2017. Upon early adoption of ASU 2017-12, together with a qualitative and quantitative analysis performed by the Bank of expected hedge effectiveness, the Bank has reversed the ineffective portion of the hedge previously recognized as a charge to earnings as of end for the three-month period ended June 30, 2017 effective September 30, 2017.
